(declare-fun i_loop () (_ BitVec 22))
(declare-fun i-loop () Int)
(assert (and (> i-loop 0) (< i-loop 21)))
(assert (= ((_ int2bv 22) i-loop) i_loop))
(define-fun getbit ((x (_ BitVec 22)) (index (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 1)
    ((_ extract 0 0) (bvlshr x index)))
    
(define-fun reverse ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (concat((_ extract 0 0)x)(concat((_ extract 1 1)x)(concat((_ extract 2 2)x)(concat((_ extract 3 3)x)(concat((_ extract 4 4)x)(concat((_ extract 5 5)x)(concat((_ extract 6 6)x)(concat((_ extract 7 7)x)(concat((_ extract 8 8)x)(concat((_ extract 9 9)x)(concat((_ extract 10 10)x)(concat((_ extract 11 11)x)(concat((_ extract 12 12)x)(concat((_ extract 13 13)x)(concat((_ extract 14 14)x)(concat((_ extract 15 15)x)(concat((_ extract 16 16)x)(concat((_ extract 17 17)x)(concat((_ extract 18 18)x)(concat((_ extract 19 19)x)(concat ((_ extract 20 20)x)((_ extract 21 21)x)))))))))))))))))))))))

(define-fun loopConV ((x (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (and
        (= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 21 21) x) ) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop
        (= (getbit x (bvsub i_loop (_ bv1 22))) ((_ extract 20 20) x)))) ;; k ~ i_loop-1

(define-fun loopConF ((x (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 21 21) x))) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop

(define-fun next ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (concat (getbit (bvlshr x (_ bv1 22)) i_loop) ((_ extract 21 1) x)))

(define-fun yesterday ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvshl x (_ bv1 22)))

(define-fun zeta ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvor (bvshl x (_ bv1 22)) (_ bv1 22)))

(define-fun untilNL ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvor
        B
        (bvand
            A
            (bvnot
                (reverse
                    (bvadd
                        (reverse (bvor B A))
                        (reverse B)))))))

(define-fun until ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (untilNL A (concat (getbit (untilNL A B) i_loop) ((_ extract 20 0) B))))
(define-fun release ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvnot (until (bvnot A) (bvnot B))))

(define-fun since ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvor
        B
        (bvand
            A
            (bvnot
                (bvadd
                    (bvor B A)
                    B)))))

(define-fun trigger ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvnot (since (bvnot A) (bvnot B))))

(define-fun alw ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    ((_ repeat 22) (bvredand x)))

(define-fun som ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    ((_ repeat 22) (bvredor x)))

(define-fun alwfNL ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvand
        x
        (reverse
            (bvsub
                (reverse (bvnot x))
                (_ bv1 22)))))

(define-fun alwf ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (alwfNL (concat (getbit (alwfNL x) i_loop) ((_ extract 20 0) x))))

(define-fun alwp ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvand
        x
        (bvsub
            (bvnot x)
            (_ bv1 22))))

(define-fun somfNL ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvor
        x
        (bvnot
            (reverse
                (bvsub
                    (reverse x)
                    (_ bv1 22))))))

(define-fun somf ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (somfNL (concat (getbit (somfNL x) i_loop) ((_ extract 20 0) x))))

(define-fun somp ((x (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvor
        x
        (bvnot
            (bvsub
                x
                (_ bv1 22)))))
(define-fun bviff ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvxnor A B))
